               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF (NOT PrintSummary AND NOT PrintDetails) THEN

                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CASE TRUE OF
                                    (PrintSummary AND PrintDetails):
                                      IF NOT (Number IN [1,2]) THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    (PrintSummary AND NOT PrintDetails):
                                      IF Number = 2 THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    (NOT PrintSummary AND PrintDetails):
                                      IF Number = 1 THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                  END;
                                END;

    { 1100525012;2;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012047;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Cost Type,Cost Object)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF (NOT PrintDetails) AND (CopyLoop.Number = 2) THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               ActualCost2 := 0;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  PrevControlProjectCostObject@1100528500 : Record 11012047;
                                  PrevCostControlManagement@1100528501 : Codeunit 11012006;
                                BEGIN
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Period Filter", "Period Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Cumulation Filter", "Cumulation Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Prognosis Filter", "Prognosis Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Progress Filter", "Progress Filter");

                                  SETFILTER("Purchase Action Filter", '<>%1', '');
                                  CALCFIELDS(Purchase, "Actual Costs");
                                  MatchedToOrders := "Actual Costs";

                                  SETRANGE("Purchase Action Filter");

                                  CostControlManagement.CalcFieldsCostObj("Control Project/Cost Object");
                                  PurchBudget := "Purchase Budget";
                                  ExtensionOption := Extension + Options;
                                  OrgBudgetAmount := "Original Budget Amount";
                                  ActualCost := "Actual Costs";
                                  IF "Cost Type" = "Cost Type"::Labor
                                    THEN ActualCost2 += ActualCost;
                                  PrognosisTotalCost2 := "Prognosis Total Cost";
                                  ExpectedCost := PrognosisTotalCost2 - ActualCost;
                                  RiscCoveragePrognosis := "Risc Coverage (Prognosis)";
                                  TotalBudget := Budget;
                                  Adjustments := Adjustments;
                                  OpenPurchase := "Open (Purchase)" + "Received/Not Invoiced";

                                  CostControlManagement.AllowedAndPurchCostObj(
                                    "Control Project/Cost Object", Allowed, AllowedHours, PrevAllowed,
                                    PrevAllowedHours, PurchaseAmount, PurchResult, PurchCost,
                                    ActualPurchResult, TotPurchResult, TRUE);


                                  PurchResult := PurchResult - ("Risc Coverage" - "Risc Coverage Withdraw");

                                  PrognEndResult := CostControlManagement.PrognEndResultCostObj("Control Project/Cost Object", TRUE);

                                  PrevControlProjectCostObject.GET("Project No.", "Cost Type", "Cost Object");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Period Filter", PrevControlProjectCostObject."Period Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Cumulation Filter", PrevControlProjectCostObject."Cumulation Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER(PrevPrognosisFilter, PrevControlProjectCostObject."Prognosis Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Progress Filter", PrevControlProjectCostObject."Progress Filter");
                                  PrevCostControlManagement.CalcFieldsCostObj(PrevControlProjectCostObject);
                                  PrevPrognEndResult := PrevCostControlManagement.PrognEndResultCostObj(PrevControlProjectCostObject, TRUE);
                                  IF PrevPrognEndResult <> 0 THEN
                                    PrognDifference := PrognEndResult - PrevPrognEndResult
                                  ELSE
                                    PrognDifference := 0;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Job;
               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525050;3;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11020604;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Prognosis Date,Start Date)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               LiquidityPrognosisProjLine@1100525000 : Record 11020604;
                             BEGIN
                               LiquidityPrognosisProjLine.SETFILTER("Project No.", Job."No.");
                               IF LiquidityPrognosisProjLine.FINDLAST THEN
                                 "Liquidity Prognosis Proj Line".SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", LiquidityPrognosisProjLine."Prognosis Date");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  JobLedgerEntry@1100529700 : Record 11072005;
                                  StartDate@1100529701 : Date;
                                  EndDate@1100529702 : Date;
                                BEGIN
                                  RevenuesFilterPeriod := 0;
                                  JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.", "Posting Date");
                                  JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", Job."No.");
                                  JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Main Project No.", Job."Main Project");
                                  JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type", JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Sale);
                                  JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Advance Payment", FALSE);
                                  JobLedgerEntry.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                                  StartDate := "Liquidity Prognosis Proj Line"."Start Date";
                                  IF StartDate <> 0D THEN BEGIN
                                    EndDate := CALCDATE('<+1M-1D>', StartDate);
                                    JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date", StartDate, EndDate);
                                  END
                                  ELSE
                                    JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date", StartDate);

                                  IF JobLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                    REPEAT
                                      RevenuesFilterPeriod -= JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
                                    UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Job;
               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(No.) }

  CODE
  {
    VAR
      Permissions@1100525047 : Codeunit 11012026;
      DeterminePrognosisDate@1100525045 : Codeunit 11012029;
      CostControlManagement@1100525044 : Codeunit 11012006;
      DateSelectionManagement@1100525043 : Codeunit 11130005;
      PeriodFilter@1100525042 : Text[250];
      ActualCost@1100525015 : Decimal;
      PrognEndResult@1100525009 : Decimal;
      Text002@1100525050 : TextConst 'DEU=Periode auf Registerkarte ≥Option  auswÑhlen.;ENU=Select period on option tab.;NLD=Geef periodeselectie in onder optie tabblad.;NOR=Velg periode pÜ valgfanen;SVE=VÑlj period pÜ alternativfliken.';
      ExtensionOption@1100525051 : Decimal;

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF Job.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Job.TABLECAPTION, Job.GETFILTERS));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcProject@1100525005();
    VAR
      PrognosisLocal@1100528500 : Record 11012034;
      PrognosisLine@1100528501 : Record 11012035;
      I@1100525000 : Integer;
      Counter@1100525001 : Integer;
      JobLedgerEntry@1100525003 : Record 11072005;
      CustLedgerEntry@1100525002 : Record 21;
      ExtensionContract@1100525008 : Record 11012004;
      Option@1100525007 : Record 11012502;
      ProjectInstallment@1100525009 : Record 11012018;
      MainProjFilter@1100525005 : Text[30];
      ProjFilter@1100525004 : Text[30];
      PeriodDiff@1100525006 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      PrognosisLocal.RESET;
      PrognosisLocal.SETRANGE("Project No.", Job."No.");
      PrognosisLocal.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", 0D, Job."Prognosis Filter");
      Counter := PrognosisLocal.COUNT;

      IF Counter >= 5 THEN
        I := 5
      ELSE
        I := Counter;

      CLEAR(PrognosisDate);
      CLEAR(PrognosisTotalCost);
      PrognosisLocal.ASCENDING(FALSE);
      IF PrognosisLocal.FINDSET THEN
        WHILE I > 0 DO BEGIN
          PrognosisLocal.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Total Cost");
          PrognosisDate[I] := PrognosisLocal."Prognosis Date";
          // PrognosisTotalCost[I] := Prognosis3."Prognosis Total Cost";
          PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", PrognosisLocal."Project No.");
          PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", PrognosisLocal."Prognosis Date");
          IF PrognosisLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            PrognosisLine.CALCFIELDS("Total Prognosis End Result");
            PrognosisTotalCost[I] := PrognosisLine."Total Prognosis End Result";
          END;
          PrognosisLocal.NEXT;
          I -= 1;
        END;

      IF Job."Single/Main/Sub Project" <> Job."Single/Main/Sub Project"::"Main Project" THEN BEGIN
        MainProjFilter := '';
        ProjFilter := Job."No.";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        MainProjFilter := Job."No.";
        ProjFilter := '';
      END;
      Job.SETFILTER("Project Filter", ProjFilter);
      Job.CALCFIELDS("Contract Amount", Revenues, "Hours Budget", "Labor Budget", "Actual Hours", "Actual Costs");
      HoursBudget := Job."Hours Budget";
      LaborBudget := Job."Labor Budget";
      IF HoursBudget <> 0 THEN
        BudgetPercent := LaborBudget/HoursBudget;
      ActualHours := Job."Actual Hours";
      ActualCosts := Job."Actual Costs";
      // ActualCost2 := ActualCosts - ActualCost;
      IF ActualHours <> 0 THEN
        ActualPercent := ActualCost2/ActualHours;

      Revenues := Job.Revenues;

      NotPaid := 0;
      NotOverDue := 0;
      Less30day := 0;
      Less60day := 0;
      Less90day := 0;
      More90day := 0;

      CustLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Customer No.","Posting Date","Currency Code");
      CustLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Document Type", '%1|%2',
        CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::Invoice, CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
      CustLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Project No.",ProjFilter);
      CustLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", Job.GETFILTER("Cumulation Filter"));
      CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE(Open, TRUE);
      IF CustLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
        CustLedgerEntry.CALCFIELDS("Amount (LCY)", "Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
        NotPaid += (CustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
        PeriodDiff := TODAY - CustLedgerEntry."Due Date";
          CASE TRUE OF
            PeriodDiff <= 0 :
              NotOverDue += CustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)";
            (PeriodDiff > 0) AND (PeriodDiff <= 30) :
              Less30day += CustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)";
            (PeriodDiff > 30) AND (PeriodDiff <= 60) :
              Less60day += CustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)";
            (PeriodDiff > 60) AND (PeriodDiff <= 90) :
              Less90day += CustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)";
            PeriodDiff > 90 :
              More90day += CustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)";
          END;
      UNTIL CustLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;

      ExtensionToInvoice := 0;
      ExtensionApproved := 0;
      ExtensionContract.RESET;
      ExtensionContract.SETFILTER("Project No.", ProjFilter);
      ExtensionContract.SETFILTER("Main Project No.", MainProjFilter);
      ExtensionContract.SETFILTER("Contract Date", Job.GETFILTER("Cumulation Filter"));
      IF ExtensionContract.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF ExtensionContract.Status = ExtensionContract.Status::"Invoicing Allowed" THEN
            ExtensionToInvoice := ExtensionToInvoice + ExtensionContract."Contract Amount (LCY)";
          IF ExtensionContract.Status = ExtensionContract.Status::Order THEN
            ExtensionApproved :=  ExtensionApproved + ExtensionContract."Contract Amount (LCY)";
        UNTIL ExtensionContract.NEXT = 0;

      OptionToInvoice := 0;
      OptionApproved := 0;
      Option.RESET;
      Option.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.", "Plot No.", Group, "Sub Group", "Contract Date");
      Option.SETFILTER("Project No.", ProjFilter);
      Option.SETFILTER("Main Project No.", MainProjFilter);
      Option.SETFILTER("Contract Date", Job.GETFILTER("Cumulation Filter"));
      Option.SETFILTER(Status, '%1..%2', Option.Status::Order, Option.Status::Invoice);
      IF Option.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          CASE Option.Status OF
            Option.Status::Order:
              OptionApproved := OptionApproved + Option."Contract Amount";
            Option.Status::Invoice:
              OptionToInvoice := OptionToInvoice + Option."Contract Amount";
          END;
        UNTIL Option.NEXT = 0;

      JobLedgerEntry.RESET;
      JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.", "Posting Date");
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Job No.", ProjFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Main Project No.", MainProjFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", Job.GETFILTER("Cumulation Filter"));
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type", JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Sale);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Advance Payment", FALSE);
      JobLedgerEntry.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
      IF JobLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          ProjectInstallment.RESET;
          IF ProjectInstallment.GET(JobLedgerEntry."Job No.", JobLedgerEntry.Principal, JobLedgerEntry."Plot No.", JobLedgerEntry."Installment No.") THEN BEGIN
            IF (ProjectInstallment."Extension Contract" <> '') OR (ProjectInstallment.Option <> '') THEN
              ExtensionsInvoiced := ExtensionsInvoiced - JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)"
            ELSE
              InstallmentsInvoiced := InstallmentsInvoiced - JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
          END ELSE
            CostPlusInvoiced -= JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)"
        UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;

      ContractAmountInclExtension := Job."Contract Amount" + ExtensionToInvoice +
        ExtensionApproved + OptionToInvoice + OptionApproved;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
</Code>
  <Language>=User!Language</Language>
  <ConsumeContainerWhitespace>true</ConsumeContainerWhitespace>
  <rd:ReportUnitType>Cm</rd:ReportUnitType>
</Report>
    END_OF_RDLDATA
  }
}
